软物质·流体·统计

Physical Mechanism behind the Early Onset of the Ultimate State in Supergravitational Centrifugal Thermal Convection

研究问题超重力离心热对流中，热湍流为何能在远低于经典 Rayleigh-Bénard 对流的 Rayleigh 数下提前进入“终极态”？核心是揭示经典态到终极态转变的触发机制：残余地球重力如何在高速旋转的环形对流腔内改变近壁边界层稳定性，并导致传热突然增强。
创新方法Aha 点是把“残余地球重力”从实验误差变成关键物理机制：地球重力垂直于离心浮力，打破上下对称性，在内冷外热圆柱壁附近诱导两条沿轴向拉伸的 Stewartson 涡层；当 Stewartson 层厚度与黏性边界层厚度相当时，两种边界层在近壁区域强耦合，扭曲原本层流型黏性边界层，触发其湍流化，从而提前进入终极传热态。
工作流程输入为高速旋转圆柱环隙装置：内圆柱冷却、外圆柱加热，改变转速与温差得到不同 Froude 数 Fr 和 Rayleigh 数 Ra；实验测量热输入并计算 Nusselt 数 Nu，绘制 Nu-Ra 与补偿曲线以识别转变点；用样条插值确定临界 Ra*；再通过三维直接数值模拟提取近壁轴向速度与方位速度剖面，分别计算 Stewartson 层厚度 δst 和黏性边界层厚度 δν；最后用尺度关系 δst/L∼Fr⁻¹/6、δν/L∼Ra⁻¹/4 推导并验证 Ra*∼Fr²/3。
关键结果实验覆盖 Fr=1.78–56.2、Ra=1.76×10⁹–3.04×10¹¹，发现传热标度从经典态 Nu∼Ra⁰.27 突变为终极态 Nu∼Ra⁰.46；临界 Rayleigh 数随 Froude 数增大而升高，满足 Ra*∼Fr²/3，例如 Fr=1.78 时 Ra*约为 9×10⁹，而 Fr=56.2 时接近 8×10¹⁰；归一化后不同 Fr 数据坍缩成两条主曲线；数值模拟显示 δst/δν 随 Fr⁻¹/6Ra¹/4 增长，临界转变时 δst/δν 平均约 0.78，接近边界层厚度相当的理论判据。
应用价值该研究给出了终极热湍流提前出现的可视化物理图像：残余重力诱导的 Stewartson 层像一把近壁“扰动刀片”，切入黏性边界层并促使其湍流化；这为在实验室实现极端天体、地幔、大气和旋转工程设备中的高 Rayleigh 数热对流提供了机制依据，也为旋转换热器、涡轮机械腔体、强离心场热管理等系统中利用边界层耦合增强传热提供设计思路。
展开精读
## 第一部分：核心概览 该研究揭示了超重力离心热对流中**终极态湍流提前出现**的物理机制：残余地球重力在冷热圆柱壁附近诱导**Stewartson 层**，当其厚度与**黏性边界层**相当时，两类边界层强耦合并扰动原本层流型边界层，触发向湍流边界层转变，从而使传热指数由经典态的 **γ = 0.27** 跃升至终极态的 **γ = 0.46**。实验覆盖 **Fr = 1.78–56.2**、**Raᵣ = 1.76×10⁹–3.04×10¹¹**，并发现临界 Rayleigh 数满足 **Raᵣ* ∼ Fr²/³**。该结果把离心对流中低阈值终极态从经验观测推进到边界层相互作用机制解释，补足了经典 RBC 中长期存在的转捩机制缺口。 --- ## 第二部分：结构化快速回顾 《Physical Mechanism behind the Early Onset of the Ultimate State in Supergravitational Centrifugal Thermal Convection》（Lei Ren, Jun Zhong, Rushi Lai, and Chao Sun，2026） ### 背景 热湍流在地幔、大气和工业旋转腔体中广泛存在。经典 Rayleigh-Bénard convection 难以在实验室达到地球物理和天体物理尺度的极高 **Ra**，而离心热对流通过旋转产生沿温度梯度方向的有效重力，可进入更高 **Ra**。此前已经观测到离心对流中终极态出现在 **Ra* = O(10¹⁰)**，显著低于经典 RBC 的 **Ra* = O(10¹²–10¹⁴)**，但提前转捩机制尚不清楚。 ### 方法 采用圆柱环隙离心对流装置：内壁冷却、外壁加热，整体绕竖直轴固体旋转。几何参数为 **Rᵢ = 120 mm**、**Rₒ = 240 mm**、**H = 120 mm**、**L = 120 mm**、**η = 0.5**、**Γ = 1**。工作流体为 **Silicone oil-1cs**，**Pr = 16.4**。共进行 **60 组实验**，覆盖 **ΔT = 2.77–21.35 K**、**Raᵣ = 1.76×10⁹–3.04×10¹¹**、转速 **94–528 rpm**、等效重力 **1.78g–56.2g**。同时进行三维直接数值模拟，低 **Raᵣ** 范围为 **10⁶–4.64×10⁸**。 ### 结果 低 **Raᵣ** 区域传热遵循 **Nu ∼ Raᵣ⁰.27**，对应经典态；高 **Raᵣ** 区域传热指数增大到 **γ = 0.46**，与终极态理论趋势一致。转捩在所有 **Fr** 下稳健出现，但临界 **Raᵣ*** 随 **Fr** 降低而降低：例如 **Fr = 1.78** 时 **Raᵣ* ≈ 9×10⁹**，**Fr = 56.2** 时 **Raᵣ* ≈ 8×10¹⁰**。实验得到 **Raᵣ* ∼ Fr²/³**。 ### 讨论 残余地球重力打破纯离心对流的上下对称性，在冷热圆柱壁附近产生轴向涡结构和 **Stewartson layers**。理论关系为 **δₛₜ/L ∼ Ek¹/³**，实验条件下 **Ek ∼ Fr⁻¹/²**，因此 **δₛₜ/L ∼ Fr⁻¹/⁶**；黏性边界层厚度满足 **δ_ν/L ∼ Ra⁻¹/⁴**。令 **δₛₜ ∼ δ_ν** 得到 **Ra* ∼ Fr²/³**，与实验完全一致。DNS 得到 **δₛₜ/δ_ν = 0.0021 Fr⁻¹/⁶ Raᵣ⁰.26**，指数 **0.26** 接近理论 **1/4**。 ### 局限 DNS 只能达到 **Raᵣ = 10⁶–4.64×10⁸**，低于实验转捩区间；边界层耦合机制主要依赖低 **Raᵣ** 外推和尺度一致性。高 **Raᵣ** 下直接解析 Stewartson 层与黏性边界层仍然困难，实验面临边界层厚度极小、测量分辨率不足的问题，三维 DNS 面临计算量过大问题。 ### 结论 离心对流终极态提前出现的关键不是单纯的离心浮力增强，而是**残余地球重力诱导的 Stewartson 层与黏性边界层相互作用**。当 **δₛₜ/δ_ν ≈ 0.78** 时，边界层稳定性由单一黏性边界层控制转为耦合边界层控制，局部速度各向异性增强，层流边界层失稳并转为湍流，热边界层被持续扰动，传热显著增强。 --- ## 第三部分：逐章节冷凝解析 # Physical Mechanism behind the Early Onset of the Ultimate State in Supergravitational Centrifugal Thermal Convection ## Abstract ### **Combined experiment–simulation strategy identifies the transition mechanism** 核心贡献建立在**实验测量**与**直接数值模拟**结合之上，目标是解析超重力离心对流中从**经典态 classical regime**到**终极态 ultimate regime**的转变。摘要明确写道：*"We present a combined experimental and numerical investigation of the transition from the classical to the ultimate regime of thermal turbulence in a supergravitational centrifugal convection system."* 这一表述限定了问题对象：不是一般 RBC，而是**supergravitational centrifugal convection system**；不是单纯传热标度测量，而是**transition mechanism**。 ### **Critical Rayleigh number decreases as Froude number decreases** 转捩阈值对 **Froude number Fr** 敏感，且呈系统变化：**Fr 越小，Ra* 越低**。摘要中给出的关键事实是：*"the critical Rayleigh number decreasing systematically as the Froude number, defined as the ratio of centrifugal to Earth's gravity, decreases, highlighting the effect of residual gravity."* 这里 **Fr** 被定义为**离心加速度与地球重力之比**，因此低 **Fr** 意味着残余地球重力相对更强。 ### **Stewartson layer–viscous boundary layer interaction triggers ultimate-state onset** 转捩发生在 **Stewartson layer** 厚度与**黏性边界层 viscous boundary layer**厚度相当时。摘要中的机制链条非常明确：*"Once the Rayleigh number reaches the transition threshold, the Stewartson layer induced by residual Earth gravity becomes comparable in thickness to the viscous boundary layer, and their interaction results in a coupled flow that distorts the viscous boundary layer, triggering its transition from laminar to turbulent flow and leading to a sharp increase in heat transport."* 关键逻辑为：残余重力 → Stewartson 层 → 与黏性边界层厚度匹配 → 耦合流 → 黏性边界层畸变 → 层流到湍流 → 传热跃升。 --- ## Introduction ### **Thermal turbulence requires asymptotic scaling because natural systems exceed laboratory Ra** 热驱动湍流广泛存在于自然与工程系统中，但地球物理和天体物理流动的驱动强度远高于实验可达范围，因此需要依赖高 **Ra** 极限的标度理论。开篇指出：*"Turbulent flows driven by thermal forcing are ubiquitous in nature [1,2] and in industrial processes [3]."* 随后强调实验局限：*"In geophysical and astrophysical systems, the driving strength of these flows reaches extremely high values that cannot be reproduced in laboratory experiments."* 这构成了研究终极态的根本动机。 ### **Rayleigh-Bénard convection provides the canonical framework** 经典 **Rayleigh-Bénard convection, RBC** 是研究热对流湍流的标准模型，其几何为上下水平板夹持流体，下热上冷。原文定义为：*"Rayleigh-Bénard convection (RBC), which consists of a fluid layer confined between two horizontal plates, heated from below and cooled from above."* 在该框架中，**Nusselt number Nu** 度量无量纲传热，**Rayleigh number Ra** 度量浮力驱动强度：*"the relation between the Nusselt number Nu (a dimensionless measure of convective heat transport) and the Rayleigh number Ra (a dimensionless measure of buoyancy driving) provides a powerful framework for exploring these flows."* ### **Ultimate-regime theory predicts effective exponent above 1/3 and asymptotic approach to 1/2** Kraichnan 的经典预言给出终极态传热标度 **Nu ∼ Ra¹/²(ln Ra)⁻³/²**。原文写道：*"Kraichnan [8] first predicted that, at sufficiently large Ra, turbulent flow enters the so-called ultimate regime, in which the Nusselt number scales as Nu ∼ Ra¹/² (ln Ra)⁻³/²."* 新近 Shishkina–Lohse 模型纳入 **Prandtl number Pr** 并满足严格上界条件：*"yielding the scaling relation Nu ∼ Pr±¹/² Ra¹/² (log Ra)⁻², with a negative exponent (-1/2) for Pr ≥ 1 and a positive exponent (+1/2) for Pr ≤ 1."* 两类理论的共同预测为：终极态有效指数 **γ > 1/3**，并在极高 **Ra** 下趋近 **1/2**：*"Both models predict that the effective scaling exponent γ in the relation Nu ∼ Ra^γ exceeds 1/3 in the ultimate regime... and asymptotically approaches 1/2 at very large Ra."* ### **Classical RBC has struggled to provide decisive broad-range evidence** 过去 60 年终极态是否存在一直存在争论，涉及理论与实验大量工作。原文概括为：*"Over the past 60 years, the existence of the ultimate regime has been the subject of intensive debate and extensive investigation in theory [8-15] and in laboratory experiments [11,13,16-23]."* 经典 RBC 的主要问题是难以达到足够高 **Ra** 并在宽范围内获得令人信服证据：*"in classical RBC systems, where Earth's gravity is aligned with the temperature gradient, it remains challenging to reach extremely high Ra and to obtain convincing evidence across a wide Ra range."* ### **Centrifugal convection bypasses the Ra limitation by using centrifugal acceleration as effective gravity** 超重力离心对流 **centrifugal convection, CC** 通过旋转产生沿温度梯度方向的离心加速度，而地球重力垂直于温度梯度。原文写道：*"Jiang et al. [22] introduced a supergravitational centrifugal convection (CC) system, in which centrifugal acceleration acts as an effective gravity parallel to the temperature gradient, while Earth's gravity is perpendicular to it."* 这一几何配置允许实验达到更高 **Ra**，并已经在超过一个数量级的 **Ra** 范围内提供终极态直接证据：*"The configuration of CC enables access to much larger Ra and has provided direct evidence for the existence of the ultimate regime over more than a decade in Ra [23]."* ### **CC differs fundamentally from rotating RBC in rotation-axis geometry** 离心对流与旋转 RBC **RRBC** 虽然都涉及旋转，但旋转轴与温度梯度相对方向不同。原文强调：*"the key difference is the direction of the rotation axis and the temperature gradient."* 在 RRBC 中，旋转轴、温度梯度与浮力方向一致，强旋转显著抑制对流；在 CC 中，强旋转对传热影响较小：*"In RRBC, the rotation axis is aligned with the temperature gradient as well as the buoyancy, in which a strong rotation has a great depression on convection [34], but has little effect on the heat transport in CC [22]."* 因此两者流动结构不同：*"the flow structures, i.e., the boundary zonal flow and the Taylor columns in RRBC, are different from those in CC."* ### **The unresolved problem is why CC reaches the ultimate regime much earlier than RBC** 核心科学问题是离心对流为何在 **Ra* = O(10¹⁰)** 就进入终极态，而经典 RBC 需 **Ra* = O(10¹²–10¹⁴)**。原文提出：*"what physical mechanisms govern this transition, and why does it occur at a much lower threshold in the CC system [Ra* = O(10¹⁰)] [22,23] than in the classical RBC system [Ra* = O(10¹²⁻¹⁴)] [7,13,21]?"* 这也是全文的中心创新点。 ### **Residual Earth gravity induces Stewartson layers that may destabilize boundary layers** 近期工作显示地球重力会在 CC 中诱导冷热壁附近的 **Stewartson layers**。原文写道：*"Lai et al. [36] investigated the influence of Earth's gravity on turbulent flow in the CC system and demonstrated that the Stewartson layers [37,38] forming near the inner (cooled) and outer (heated) cylinders are induced by Earth's gravity."* 终极态转捩理论上对应**层流型 Prandtl-Blasius 边界层**转为**湍流型 Prandtl-von Kármán 边界层**：*"During the transition from the classical to the ultimate regimes, the laminar-type Prandtl-Blasius boundary layer is expected to evolve into the turbulent-type Prandtl-von Kármán boundary layer through the non-normal-nonlinear mechanism."* 因此，Stewartson 层与黏性边界层的相互作用可能是关键：*"the interaction between the Stewartson layers and the viscous boundary layers near the inner (cooled) and outer (heated) cylinders may play a critical role in this transition."* ### **The measured transition is robust and Fr-dependent** 实验观察到 **Nu ∼ Ra⁰.27** 的经典态转为 **γ = 0.46** 的终极态，并且这种转变在宽 **Fr** 范围稳健存在。原文给出：*"the transition from the classical regime, characterized by an effective scaling of Nu ∼ Ra⁰.²⁷, to the ultimate regime, with a much steeper effective exponent γ = 0.46, is robust in the CC system across a wide range of Froude numbers."* 临界 **Ra** 随 **Fr** 降低而降低，说明残余重力影响转捩：*"the critical Rayleigh number for the onset of the ultimate regime decreases as the Froude number decreases, revealing the influence of residual gravity."* --- ## Experimental setup ### **Annular rotating cell geometry fixes radius ratio and aspect ratio** 实验装置为圆柱环隙，内壁冷却、外壁加热，整体绕竖直轴固体旋转。原文描述为：*"This experimental setup is a cylindrical annulus with a cooled inner wall and a heated outer wall under a solid-body rotation around its vertical axis."* 几何尺寸非常明确：内冷壁外半径 **Rᵢ = 120 mm**，外热壁内半径 **Rₒ = 240 mm**，高度 **H = 120 mm**，环隙宽度 **L = 120 mm**，半径比 **η = 0.5**，纵横比 **Γ = 1**。对应原文：*"The outer (inner) radius of the cooled inner (heated outer) wall is Rᵢ = 120 mm (Rₒ = 240 mm) and the height of the cylindrical annulus is H = 120 mm, resulting in a gap of L = Rₒ - Rᵢ = 120 mm, a radius ratio of η = Rᵢ / Rₒ = 0.5, and an aspect ratio of Γ = H / L = 1."* ### **Froude number quantifies the strength of centrifugal acceleration relative to Earth gravity** 为研究残余重力作用，引入 **Froude number Fr = Ω²Rₘ/g**。其物理含义是离心加速度相对于地球重力的大小。原文定义为：*"one can take the Froude number Fr = Ω² Rₘ / g as another dimensionless parameter that is a measure of the centrifugal acceleration compared to the gravitational acceleration."* 低 **Fr** 表示地球重力相对离心力更重要，因此更容易观察重力诱导的 Stewartson 层效应。 ### **Silicone oil-1cs is chosen to resolve the transition window** 工作流体为 **Silicone oil-1cs**，用于测定经典态到终极态的临界 **Raᵣ***。原文写道：*"We use Silicone oil-1cs (Shin-Etsu Chemical Co., Ltd.) as the working fluid to investigate the critical Rayleigh number Raᵣ^* for the transition from the classical to the ultimate regime."* End Matter 给出其 **25°C** 物性：**α = 1.29×10⁻³ K⁻¹**、**ν = 1.00×10⁻⁶ m² s⁻¹**、**κ = 6.11×10⁻⁸ m² s⁻¹**、**λ = 0.10 W(mK)⁻¹**、**Pr = 16.4**。 --- ## Measurement results ### **Heat transport shows classical scaling at low Ra and ultimate-regime scaling at high Ra** 图 1(a) 展示 **Fr = 1.78–56.2** 范围内 **Nu–Raᵣ** 关系。低 **Raᵣ** 区域满足 **Nu ∼ Raᵣ⁰.27**，与经典态一致：*"In the low-Raᵣ regime, the data follow an effective scaling of Nu ∼ Raᵣ⁰.²⁷ (solid red line), consistent with the previous study [23], indicating that the system is in the classical regime."* 高 **Raᵣ** 区域与终极态理论一致，包括 Shishkina–Lohse 标度 **Nu ∼ Pr⁻¹/²Raᵣ¹/²(log Raᵣ₎⁻²** 和 Kraichnan 标度 **Nu ∼ Raᵣ¹/²(ln Raᵣ₎⁻³/²**：*"In the high-Raᵣ regime, the data agree with the theoretical predictions for the ultimate regime... exhibiting a steep effective scaling exponent within the current parameter range."* ### **Compensated plots reveal a robust transition from γ < 1/3 to γ > 1/3** 通过绘制 **Nu/Raᵣ¹/³** 补偿图，转捩可见性增强。原文写道：*"For better visibility of the onset, Fig. 1(b) shows the plots compensated by Raᵣ¹/³."* 经典态与终极态的判据是有效指数跨越 **1/3**：*"The transition from the classical to the ultimate regime is robust across all Fr, as evidenced by the change in the effective scaling exponent from γ < 1/3 to γ > 1/3."* 这避免了仅依赖绝对 **Nu** 的判断，而使用了标度指数变化作为状态转变标志。 ### **Critical Ra depends strongly on Fr** 临界 **Raᵣ*** 随 **Fr** 显著改变。原文给出两个代表数值：*"For example, Raᵣ^* is approximately 9 × 10⁹ for Fr = 1.78, while for Fr = 56.2, it is close to 8 × 10¹⁰."* 这说明相对更强的残余地球重力使终极态更早出现。其物理解释与非正规-非线性转捩一致：*"The exact onset of the steeper scaling, corresponding to the ultimate turbulence regime, depends on Fr, consistent with the view that the transition is of a non-normal-nonlinear nature... and is sensitive to perturbations induced by Earth-gravity-driven flow in the current case."* ### **Spline interpolation defines the critical Rayleigh number objectively** 临界点提取采用 **n ≥ 3** 个转捩附近数据点，在 **Nu/Raᵣ¹/³ ∼ Raᵣ** 曲线上做样条插值，插值曲线最小值定义为对应 **Raᵣ*(n)**。原文方法为：*"we adopt spline interpolation with n ≥ 3 data points near the transition on the Nu / Raᵣ¹/³ ∼ Raᵣ curve in Fig. 1(b) and identify the minimum value of each interpolation curve as the Raᵣ^*(n)."* 最终 **Raᵣ*** 取所有 **Raᵣ*(n)** 的均值，不确定度取标准差：*"The critical Raᵣ^* is obtained by the mean value of all Raᵣ^*(n), and the standard deviation is used as its associated uncertainty."* ### **The transition threshold obeys Raᵣ* ∼ Fr²/³** 图 1(c) 给出临界 **Raᵣ*** 与 **Fr** 的关系，结果为幂律 **Raᵣ* ∼ Fr²/³**。原文写道：*"the critical Raᵣ^* increases with increasing Fr, following a power law Raᵣ^* ∼ Fr²/³."* 因为 **Fr** 越大表示残余地球重力相对越弱，所以这一关系直接支持“地球重力诱导边界层扰动降低转捩阈值”的解释。 ### **Normalized data collapse onto two master curves** 用实验得到的 **Raᵣ*** 和对应 **Nu*** 对数据归一化后，不同 **Fr** 的数据塌缩到两条主曲线。原文写道：*"the data for different Fr now collapse onto two master curves: a scaling exponent of 0.27 for Raᵣ / Raᵣ^* < 1 and Nu ∼ Raᵣ⁰.⁴⁶ for Raᵣ / Raᵣ^* > 1."* 这说明不同 **Fr** 下的转捩可以通过临界尺度统一描述，具有普适标度结构：*"clearly demonstrating the universal nature of the scaling relation."* --- ## Theoretical explanation ### **Earth gravity breaks top-bottom symmetry in pure centrifugal convection** 离心对流区别于经典 RBC 的独特之处在于：离心浮力沿径向，而地球重力沿轴向，二者不共线。原文指出：*"the presence of Earth's gravitational force breaks the top-bottom symmetric structure for pure centrifugal convection without gravity."* 这种对称性破缺导致壁面附近形成轴向拉长涡结构。 ### **Earth gravity generates elongated vortices and Stewartson layers near both cylinders** 地球重力导致冷热圆柱壁附近出现两个沿壁延伸的涡结构，并形成 **Stewartson layers**。原文描述为：*"two elongated vortex structures develop along the inner (cooled) and outer (heated) cylinders, leading to Stewartson layers that form near the cold and hot walls in the r-z plane, in addition to the viscous boundary layer in the r-φ plane."* 这里存在两个不同平面中的边界层：**r–φ 平面**中的黏性边界层，**r–z 平面**中的 Stewartson 层。 ### **Viscous and Stewartson layer thicknesses are diagnosed from different velocity components** 两类边界层厚度的测定基于不同速度分量。原文明确写道：*"The thickness of the viscous boundary layer, δ_ν, is determined from the mainstream azimuthal velocity component, whereas the thickness of the Stewartson layer, δₛₜ, is determined from the axial velocity component."* 因此 **δ_ν** 反映旋转主流的方位速度边界层，**δₛₜ** 反映残余重力驱动的轴向流边界层。 ### **Stewartson layer thickness follows Ek¹/³** 此前结果显示 **δₛₜ/L ∼ Ek¹/³**，与 RRBC 中 Stewartson 层理论一致。原文写道：*"the dimensionless thickness of the Stewartson layer in CC, δₛₜ / L, is governed by rotational effects, with δₛₜ / L ∼ Ek¹ / ³, consistent with results obtained in the RRBC system."* 其中 **Ek = ν/(ΩH²)** 表征 Coriolis 力影响：*"Here, Ek = ν / (Ω H²⁾ is the Ekman number, which characterizes the influence of the Coriolis force."* ### **Experimental fixed-fluid conditions imply Ek ∼ Fr⁻¹/²** 在固定 **ν, H, Rₘ, g** 的实验中，**Ek** 与 **Fr** 都只依赖角速度 **Ω**。原文给出定义：*"Ek = ν/(Ω H²⁾, Fr = Ω² Rₘ/g."* 因此有：*"both Ek and Fr only depend on Ω; then we can obtain the practical relationship between Ek and Fr in the experiments: Ek ∼ Fr⁻¹/²."* 进而得到：*"δₛₜ / L ∼ Ek¹/³ ∼ Fr⁻¹/⁶."* ### **Viscous boundary layer thickness scales as Ra⁻¹/⁴** 在 RBC 或 CC 中，采用 **Re ∼ Ra¹/²**，并用边界层关系 **δ_ν/L ∼ Re⁻¹/²**，得到 **δ_ν/L ∼ Ra⁻¹/⁴**。原文写道：*"according to Re ∼ Ra¹/², the thickness of the viscous boundary layer δ_ν follows δ_ν / L ∼ Re⁻¹/² ∼ Ra⁻¹/⁴."* 这意味着随着 **Ra** 增大，黏性边界层变薄。 ### **Comparable boundary-layer thickness predicts Ra* ∼ Fr²/³** 核心理论假设是经典态到终极态的转捩发生在 **δ_ν** 与 **δₛₜ** 厚度相当时。原文表述为：*"assuming that the transition from the classical regime to the ultimate regime occurs when the thicknesses of the viscous boundary layer δ_ν and the Stewartson layer δₛₜ are comparable in scale."* 令 **Ra⁻¹/⁴ ∼ Fr⁻¹/⁶**，得到 **Ra* ∼ Fr²/³**：*"Ra⁻¹/⁴ ∼ Fr⁻¹/⁶ ⇒ Ra^* ∼ Fr²/³, which is in full agreement with the present experimental data."* 这一推导把实验幂律与边界层尺度匹配直接连接起来。 --- ## Physical mechanism ### **Layer-thickness coincidence creates strongly coupled near-wall velocity components** 当 **Stewartson 层**与**黏性边界层**厚度相当时，两者速度分量在壁面附近强耦合，形成耦合流。原文提出：*"When the thicknesses of the Stewartson layer and the viscous boundary layer coincide, their velocity components strongly couple near the inner and outer cylinders, forming a coupled flow that can distort the viscous boundary layer and enhance the anisotropy of local velocity variations."* 这里的关键不是单一边界层变薄，而是不同方向速度分量在同一壁面尺度内相互作用。 ### **Coupled flow destabilizes the laminar viscous boundary layer and enhances heat transport** 耦合流导致黏性边界层畸变，触发流动不稳定，最终使层流边界层破裂成湍流边界层。原文给出的完整链条是：*"This interaction can trigger flow instability, eventually leading to the breakdown of the laminar boundary layer into turbulence."* 随后湍流边界层持续扰动热边界层，使传热增强：*"The turbulent boundary layer continuously disturbs the thermal boundary layer, characterized by a significant increase in heat transport."* ### **The mechanism is analogous to boundary-layer control in rotating RBC** 这一解释与 King 等人在 RRBC 中发现的边界层厚度竞争机制类似。原文写道：*"This mechanism is similar to that reported by King et al. [25], who found that the transition between rotationally dominated and nonrotating behavior in RRBC is controlled by the relative thicknesses of the thermal (nonrotating) and Ekman (rotating) boundary layers."* 相似性在于：宏观流态转变由不同边界层厚度相对大小控制；差异在于 CC 中涉及的是 **Stewartson–viscous boundary layer interaction**，而 King 等涉及 **thermal–Ekman boundary layer interaction**。 ### **DNS includes gravity and no-slip top/bottom boundaries** 为检验机制，进行三维 DNS，包含地球重力与上下端盖无滑移边界。原文写道：*"we perform three-dimensional direct numerical simulations that incorporate gravity and no-slip top and bottom boundaries, within a relatively low-Raᵣ range of 10⁶ ∼ 4.64 × 10⁸."* 低 **Raᵣ** 是重要限制，因为实验转捩发生在 **10⁹–10¹¹** 量级。 ### **DNS shows δₛₜ/δ_ν increases with Raᵣ as a power law** 在固定 **Fr = 10**、外热圆柱附近，DNS 计算 **δₛₜ/δ_ν** 随 **Raᵣ** 增大而上升。原文写道：*"It is observed that the ratio δₛₜ / δ_ν increases with Raᵣ, following a power-law relation, i.e., δₛₜ / δ_ν = 0.0021Fr⁻¹ / ⁶Raᵣ⁰.²⁶."* 指数 **0.26** 接近理论预测 **1/4**：*"The scaling exponent of 0.26 is close to the theoretical prediction δₛₜ / δ_ν ∼ Ra¹ / ⁴."* ### **Experimental transition points correspond to δₛₜ/δ_ν ≈ 0.78** 将实验得到的各 **Fr** 下临界 **Raᵣ*** 代入 DNS 拟合关系，得到临界厚度比均值 **0.78**，接近 **1**。原文写道：*"Substituting the experimentally determined critical value Raᵣ^* at different Fr values into the fitted relation yields critical ratios with a mean of 0.78, which is close to 1."* 这为“厚度相当触发转捩”的尺度假设提供了量化支持。 ### **Scaling collapse confirms universal dependence on Fr⁻¹/⁶Raᵣ¹/⁴** 图 3 插图中，**δₛₜ/δ_ν** 对 **Fr⁻¹/⁶Raᵣ¹/⁴** 作图后，数据塌缩到单一直线。原文写道：*"The inset of Fig. 3 further presents δₛₜ / δ_ν as a function of Fr⁻¹ / ⁶Raᵣ¹ / ⁴, where all data points collapse onto a single line, clearly demonstrating the universal character of this scaling relationship."* 这说明控制变量确实是 Stewartson 层与黏性边界层的相对厚度，而非单独的 **Raᵣ** 或 **Fr**。 ### **Boundary-layer interaction supports the ultimate-state trigger mechanism** DNS 与理论共同支持耦合边界层扰动机制。原文总结为：*"This supports our theoretical explanation: a coupled flow structure, arising from the interaction of the Stewartson and viscous boundary layers, introduces distortions to the boundary layer flow, which in turn promotes flow instability and triggers the transition to turbulence."* 该机制把低阈值终极态与残余地球重力直接联系起来。 --- ## Conclusion and outlook ### **Heat-transport exponent increases from 0.27 to 0.46 across Fr range** 最终结果显示，在宽 **Fr** 范围内，传热标度指数从经典态 **γ = 0.27** 增大到终极态 **γ = 0.46**。原文写道：*"Across a wide range of Froude numbers, the heat transport exponent increases from γ = 0.27 to γ = 0.46, marking the transition from the classical regime to the ultimate regime."* 这一指数变化符合终极态判据 **γ > 1/3**。 ### **Lower Fr lowers the ultimate-state onset threshold** 临界 **Raᵣ*** 随 **Fr** 降低而降低，说明地球重力影响转捩。原文写道：*"The corresponding critical Rayleigh number for the onset of the ultimate regime is found to decrease with decreasing Froude number, highlighting the effect of Earth's gravity on the transition."* 这与理论关系 **Raᵣ* ∼ Fr²/³** 一致。 ### **Classical regime is controlled by the viscous boundary layer because Stewartson layer is thinner** 在经典态，地球重力诱导的 Stewartson 层比黏性边界层薄，因此边界层稳定性主要由黏性边界层控制。原文表述为：*"In the classical regime, the Stewartson layer induced by Earth's gravity is thinner than the viscous boundary layer, so the latter controls boundary-layer stability."* 这解释了低 **Raᵣ** 下为何仍保持经典态传热。 ### **Ultimate regime begins when δₛₜ/δ_ν approaches unity** 当 **Raᵣ** 达到临界值后，Stewartson 层厚度与黏性边界层相当，临界比值约 **δₛₜ/δ_ν ≈ 0.78**。原文写道：*"Once Raᵣ reaches the critical Rayleigh number, i.e., in the ultimate regime, the Stewartson layer becomes comparable to the viscous boundary layer (δₛₜ / δ_ν ≈ 0.78), and boundary-layer stability is then governed by their interaction."* 这给出了终极态提前发生的定量阈值。 ### **Strong coupling enhances anisotropy and triggers laminar-to-turbulent transition** 在终极态起点，壁面附近速度分量强耦合，产生耦合流，扭曲黏性边界层并增强局部速度变化各向异性。原文写道：*"the velocity components are strongly coupled near the walls, potentially giving rise to a coupled flow that distorts the viscous boundary layer and enhances the anisotropy of local velocity variations, thereby triggering flow instability and causing the laminar layer to transition to turbulence."* 该机制将边界层失稳与传热增强直接相连。 ### **Turbulent boundary layers disturb thermal boundary layers and increase heat transport** 层流边界层转为湍流后，热边界层受到持续扰动，导致传热显著增强。原文写道：*"The turbulent boundary layer continuously disturbs the thermal boundary layer, characterized by a significant increase in heat transport."* 这解释了 **Nu** 标度指数为何从 **0.27** 提高到 **0.46**。 ### **Current support relies on extrapolated low-Ra DNS** 机制解释受到 DNS 支持，但 DNS 发生在较低 **Raᵣ**，因此属于外推支持而非转捩条件下的直接解析。原文明确写道：*"This interpretation is supported by extrapolated results from direct numerical simulations at relatively low Raᵣ."* 这是结论中最重要的谨慎限定。 ### **Direct high-Ra boundary-layer measurement remains the key future challenge** 未来需要在转捩条件下直接测量和建模两类边界层相互作用。原文写道：*"Future work will need to directly measure and theoretically model the interaction of the boundary layers through experiments and simulations at the onset conditions, thereby providing direct evidence for this interpretation."* 实验挑战是高 **Ra** 下解析极薄边界层，数值挑战是达到足够高 **Raᵣ** 并保持三维重力效应：*"the challenge for experiments is resolving the boundary layers at such high Rayleigh numbers, while for numerical simulations, it is reaching such high Raᵣ, particularly in three-dimensional simulations to capture the additional effects of gravity."* --- ## End Matter ## Governing equations ### **The model uses Oberbeck-Boussinesq equations in a rotating reference frame** 控制方程基于**Oberbeck-Boussinesq 假设**，在旋转参考系中写出无量纲形式。原文写道：*"Dimensionless governing equations following the Oberbeck-Boussinesq assumption in a rotating reference frame can be expressed as..."* 方程包括不可压缩条件 **∇·u = 0**、温度输运方程和动量方程。温度方程为：*"∂T/∂t + ∇ · (uT) = 1/√(Raᵣ Pr) ∇²T."* ### **Momentum equation includes Coriolis force, viscosity, centrifugal buoyancy, and gravity buoyancy** 动量方程包含压力梯度、Coriolis 项、黏性扩散、径向离心浮力和轴向重力浮力。原文动量方程中出现：*"- Ro⁻¹ ê_z × u"*、*"√(Pr/Raᵣ₎ ∇²u"*、*"- [2(1 - η)/(1 + η)] r T êᵣ"* 以及 *"+ (Ra_g/Raᵣ₎ T ê_z."* 这四项分别对应旋转效应、黏性扩散、离心热浮力和地球重力热浮力。 ### **Four primary dimensionless control parameters govern the system** 关键控制参数包括 **centrifugal Rayleigh number Raᵣ**、**gravitational Rayleigh number Ra_g**、**inverse Rossby number Ro⁻¹** 和 **Prandtl number Pr**。原文写道：*"there are four key control dimensionless parameters, namely the centrifugal Rayleigh number Raᵣ, gravitational Rayleigh number Ra_g, inverse Rossby number Ro⁻¹, and Prandtl number Pr."* 定义为： - **Raᵣ = αΩ²RₘΔTL³/(νκ)** - **Ra_g = αgΔTL³/(νκ)** - **Ro⁻¹ = 2[αΔTRₘ/L]⁻¹/²** - **Pr = ν/κ** ### **Nusselt number is defined from total heat flux relative to conductive heat flux** 响应参数 **Nu** 度量系统实际热通量相对于纯导热热通量的比例。原文定义为：*"One of the response dimensionless parameters is the Nusselt number Nu, which quantifies the ratio between the heat flux transported by the system Jₜₒₜₐₗ and that by conduction J_conduction."* 公式为 **Nu = Q ln(Rₒ/Rᵢ₎/(λΔT2πH)**，其中 **Q** 是外圆柱输入功率，**λ** 是热导率，**H** 是外圆柱高度。 ### **AFiD-based numerical solver is extended to include CC physics** 数值代码基于开源 **AFiD** 扩展。原文写道：*"The code utilized in this Letter is an extended development based on the open-source program AFiD [42-44], which was originally designed for the classical RBC systems."* 在 CC 系统中加入 **Coriolis force**、**gravity** 和 **centrifugal buoyancy**：*"In the CC system, we have incorporated the effects of the Coriolis force, gravity, and centrifugal buoyancy."* ### **Boundary conditions match the annular rotating convection geometry** 内外圆柱面采用**无滑移 no-slip** 和**等温 isothermal**边界条件；上下端盖采用**无滑移**和**绝热 adiabatic**条件。原文写道：*"No-slip and isothermal boundary conditions are imposed on the inner and outer cylindrical surfaces, while no-slip and adiabatic boundary conditions are applied to the top and bottom end covers."* ### **Numerical discretization and statistics are specified quantitatively** 网格为交错网格，空间导数采用二阶中心差分，时间推进结合三阶分步 Runge-Kutta 与 Crank-Nicholson 隐式项。原文写道：*"Grid generation employs a staggered grid scheme, with spatial derivatives solved via the second-order central difference method, and temporal derivatives processed by combining the third-order fractional-step Runge-Kutta method with Crank-Nicholson implicit terms."* 显式时间推进满足 **CFL ≤ 0.8**：*"the Courant-Friedrichs-Lewy number is restricted to within 0.8."* 流场通常在超过 **150** 个无量纲时间单位后达到统计稳态，随后再模拟 **350** 个无量纲时间单位采样：*"the flow field reaches a statistically steady state after over 150 dimensionless time units... following which an additional 350 dimensionless time units... are conducted to collect data."* ### **Quarter-circumference simulations reduce cost without losing key flow structures** 由于 CC 流场在周向具有周期性，模拟域可缩小到半周甚至四分之一周。原文写道：*"Previous studies have confirmed that the flow field in the CC system exhibits periodic characteristics in the circumferential direction."* 只要计算域包含至少一对对流涡，传热和流动结构可与全周模拟相当：*"As long as the computational domain contains at least one pair of convective vortices, the heat transport and flow structures will be comparable to those from full-circumference simulations."* 因此多数模拟采用 **1/4 circumference**：*"we adopt 1/4 of the circumference as the computational domain."* --- ## Working fluid (Silicone oil-1cs) ### **Silicone oil-1cs offers a wider Raᵣ window around the transition** 选择 **Silicone oil-1cs** 的优势是，在相同温差范围内，它比水和 Novec-7200 更能覆盖经典态到终极态临界 **Raᵣ*** 附近的宽 **Raᵣ** 区间。原文写道：*"The advantage of using Silicone oil-1cs... is that, for the same range of temperature difference ΔT, it can cover a wider range of Raᵣ around the critical Raᵣ^* from the classical to the ultimate regime than water... or Novec-7200."* 其中水为 **Pr = 4.3 at 40°C**，Novec-7200 为 **Pr = 10.3 at 25°C**，Silicone oil-1cs 为 **Pr = 16.4 at 25°C**。 ### **Physical properties are fixed at 25°C** 表 I 给出 **Silicone oil-1cs** 在 **25°C** 下的物性。原文写道：*"Table I lists the physical properties of Silicone oil-1cs at 25°C."* 具体为：**thermal expansion α = 1.29×10⁻³ K⁻¹**，**kinematic viscosity ν = 1.00×10⁻⁶ m²s⁻¹**，**thermal diffusivity κ = 6.11×10⁻⁸ m²s⁻¹**，**thermal conductivity λ = 0.10 W(mK)⁻¹**，**Prandtl number Pr = 16.4**。 --- ## Parameter space ### **Sixty experiments cover the transition range in Fr–Raᵣ and Pr–Raᵣ planes** 参数空间在 **Fr–Raᵣ** 和 **Pr–Raᵣ** 平面中展示，总实验数为 **60**。原文写道：*"The parameter space explored in the Fr - Raᵣ and Pr - Raᵣ planes is shown in Figs. 4(a) and 4(b), respectively. A total of 60 experiments were performed."* ### **Temperature difference and Oberbeck-Boussinesq validity are controlled** 实验温差范围为 **ΔT = 2.77–21.35 K**，并满足 **Oberbeck-Boussinesq conditions**。原文写道：*"The temperature difference ΔT ranged from 2.77 to 21.35 K, and the Oberbeck-Boussinesq conditions are well satisfied."* 这意味着物性随温度变化的非 Boussinesq 效应受控，不主导观测到的转捩。 ### **Experimental Raᵣ and effective gravity ranges are broad** 实验 **Raᵣ** 覆盖 **1.76×10⁹–3.04×10¹¹**，转速为 **94–528 rpm**，对应等效重力 **1.78g–56.2g**。原文写道：*"The Rayleigh number Raᵣ spans 1.76×10⁹ to 3.04×10¹¹, and the rotation rate ranges from 94 to 528 rpm, corresponding to an effective gravity of 1.78g to 56.2g."* 这一范围足以覆盖多个 **Fr** 下的经典态—终极态转捩。 --- ## 第四部分：深度理解与语言支持 ### 1. 术语解析 #### **Ultimate regime** **Ultimate regime** 指热对流湍流中边界层也进入湍流状态的极限传热区间。经典态中体区可以湍流化，但边界层仍常保持层流型，因此 **Nu–Ra** 指数通常低于 **1/3**；终极态中边界层转为湍流，理论上有效指数超过 **1/3** 并趋近 **1/2**。文中的判断依据是 **Nu ∼ Raᵣ⁰.27** 转为 **Nu ∼ Raᵣ⁰.46**。 #### **Classical regime** **Classical regime** 不是指流动完全层流，而是指热对流整体可能已湍流，但控制传热的边界层仍是层流型或类层流型。文中低 **Raᵣ** 区域的 **γ = 0.27 < 1/3** 被归为经典态，核心原因是边界层尚未发生湍流化转捩。 #### **Stewartson layer** **Stewartson layer** 是旋转流体中因边界、剪切或几何约束产生的侧壁型边界层，通常与 Coriolis 约束和旋转效应有关。文中该层不是由离心浮力本身直接产生，而是由**残余地球重力**破坏上下对称性后，在冷热圆柱壁附近诱导的轴向涡结构形成。厚度标度为 **δₛₜ/L ∼ Ek¹/³**。 #### **Non-normal-nonlinear mechanism** **Non-normal-nonlinear mechanism** 指边界层或剪切流中，即使线性模态不具有传统指数增长，不同扰动模式也可因非正规算子产生瞬态放大，再通过非线性相互作用触发湍流。文中用它解释转捩对残余重力扰动敏感：地球重力诱导的 Stewartson 层不是简单改变平均传热，而是为边界层失稳提供有限幅值扰动通道。 #### **Compensated plot** **Compensated plot** 是将 **Nu** 除以某个参考幂律如 **Ra¹/³** 后作图，用于放大标度指数相对于参考值的偏离。若 **Nu/Ra¹/³** 随 **Ra** 下降，表示 **γ < 1/3**；若上升，表示 **γ > 1/3**。文中用该方法确定经典态到终极态的转折点。 --- ### 2. 疑难查证 #### **为什么 Fr 越小，终极态越早出现？** **Fr = Ω²Rₘ/g** 表示离心加速度相对于地球重力的强度。直觉上，离心力越强似乎越容易进入强湍流；但文中的转捩不是由体区湍流强度单独决定，而是由**边界层失稳**决定。 在固定装置和流体条件下： [ Ek = fracνØmega H², quad Fr = fracØmega²Rₘg ] 因此： [ Ek sim Fr⁻¹/² ] Stewartson 层厚度： [ δₛₜ/L sim Ek¹/³ sim Fr⁻¹/⁶ ] **Fr 越小，δₛₜ 越厚**。而黏性边界层： [ δ_ν/L sim Ra⁻¹/⁴ ] 随着 **Ra** 增大而变薄。转捩条件为： [ δₛₜ sim δ_ν ] 如果 **Fr** 较小，Stewartson 层本来就更厚，所以不需要把 **Ra** 提得很高就能与黏性边界层厚度相当。因此 **Raᵣ*** 更低。 --- #### **为什么 δₛₜ/δ_ν ≈ 0.78 而不是严格 1 也能支持机制？** 边界层“厚度相当”不是数学上必须完全相等，而是流体动力学中的尺度匹配条件。实际边界层厚度定义依赖速度剖面、阈值选取、空间位置、统计平均方法和数值分辨率。DNS 拟合关系给出的临界均值 **0.78** 接近 **O(1)**，说明 Stewartson 层与黏性边界层已经进入同一空间尺度范围，足以发生强耦合。对于湍流转捩问题，**O(1) 的厚度比**比精确等于 1 更具有物理意义。 --- #### **为什么终极态不是由 Stewartson 层本身直接等同于湍流边界层？** Stewartson 层是残余重力与旋转效应诱导的侧壁流动结构；终极态要求控制传热的边界层进入湍流型状态。二者不是同一概念。文中的机制是： 1. 地球重力诱导 **Stewartson layer**； 2. **Ra** 增大使 **viscous boundary layer** 变薄； 3. 两者厚度相当时发生速度分量强耦合； 4. 耦合流扭曲黏性边界层； 5. 黏性边界层由层流型转为湍流型； 6. 湍流边界层扰动热边界层； 7. **Nu** 显著提高，表现为终极态标度。 Stewartson 层是触发器，不是终极态本身。 --- ## 第五部分：创新评估与关联 ### 1. 创新性判断 #### **从“观察到终极态”推进到“解释为何提前出现”** 过去 2–5 年中，离心对流研究的重要进展包括 Jiang 等在 2020 年建立超重力离心热对流实验平台、2022 年给出终极态存在证据，以及 Yao 等 2025 年通过 DNS 研究从重力主导到离心主导的流动结构演化。已有工作确认 CC 能达到高 **Ra**，并显示终极态可在 **O(10¹⁰)** 出现，但缺少对转捩阈值为何远低于经典 RBC 的机制解释。 该研究的新颖性在于把提前转捩归因于**残余地球重力诱导的 Stewartson 层与黏性边界层相互作用**，而非笼统归因于离心加速度增强或实验可达更高 **Ra**。 #### **建立了可检验的临界标度 Raᵣ* ∼ Fr²/³** 最重要的理论创新是从边界层厚度标度推出： [ δₛₜ/L sim Fr⁻¹/⁶, quad δ_ν/L sim Ra⁻¹/⁴ ] 令二者相当得到： [ Raᵣ^* sim Fr²/³ ] 这一关系被实验数据验证。相比只报告 **Nu–Ra** 指数变化，这一幂律直接提供了可预测、可检验的转捩阈值模型。 #### **把地球重力从“残余误差”转化为“关键物理机制”** 在超重力离心系统中，地球重力常被视为相对离心力的小扰动，因为离心加速度可达数十倍 **g**。该研究显示，即使地球重力垂直于主要温度梯度，仍可通过诱导 Stewartson 层改变边界层稳定性，并显著降低终极态转捩阈值。这一视角改变了对“残余重力”的理解：它不是可忽略背景项，而是决定转捩阈值的核心控制因素。 #### **连接了 CC、RRBC 与经典 RBC 的边界层转捩图景** 经典 RBC 终极态转捩长期与边界层从 Prandtl-Blasius 型到 Prandtl-von Kármán 型的变化相关，但直接机制难以验证。RRBC 中已有边界层厚度竞争控制流态转变的认识。该研究将类似思想移植到 CC 中，但提出新的配对：**Stewartson layer vs viscous boundary layer**。因此，它为不同热对流系统中的转捩提供了统一思路：宏观传热态改变可由不同边界层厚度匹配和相互作用触发。 #### **实验与 DNS 的互补性构成强证据链，但仍非最终证明** 创新证据链包括： - **60 组实验**； - **Fr = 1.78–56.2**； - **Raᵣ = 1.76×10⁹–3.04×10¹¹**； - 经典态 **γ = 0.27**； - 终极态 **γ = 0.46**； - 临界标度 **Raᵣ* ∼ Fr²/³**； - DNS 拟合 **δₛₜ/δ_ν = 0.0021Fr⁻¹/⁶Raᵣ⁰.²⁶**； - 临界厚度比均值 **δₛₜ/δ_ν ≈ 0.78**。 局限在于 DNS 只覆盖 **Raᵣ = 10⁶–4.64×10⁸**，低于实验临界区间，因此边界层耦合仍需在真实转捩 **Raᵣ** 下直接验证。尽管如此，理论标度、实验临界幂律和 DNS 厚度比塌缩三者一致，使该机制具有较高可信度。
